# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# gRPC Error Status Propagation Across Go Services

## Your Task

Compare how gRPC error status codes are created and propagated in kubernetes/kubernetes vs grafana/grafana vs etcd-io/etcd. Find Go source files in each repo that create gRPC Status errors with codes (codes.NotFound, codes.Internal, etc.) and the files that translate gRPC errors to HTTP responses.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

55-assistanttext-
Perfect! I have completed the analysis of gRPC error status code propagation across the three repositories. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings

I've identified **8 critical files** and their patterns for creating and propagating gRPC error status codes:

### **etcd-io/etcd** - Pre-defined Error Mapping
- **`api/v3rpc/rpctypes/error.go`**: Pre-defines all domain-specific gRPC Status errors using `status.Error(codes.Code, message)` directly (lines 24-98)
- **`server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go`**: Maps internal errors to these pre-defined gRPC errors via `togRPCError()` function using `toGRPCErrorMap`

### **kubernetes/kubernetes** - Generic Error-to-gRPC Mapping
- **`vendor/github.com/containerd/errdefs/pkg/errgrpc/grpc.go`**: Generic mapping that converts containerd error types to gRPC codes via `statusFromError()` and `ToGRPC()`
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/kubelet/pkg/cri/streaming/errors.go`**: CRI streaming layer translates gRPC codes to HTTP status codes via `WriteError()` function
- **`vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go`**: Central mapping function `HTTPStatusFromCode()` for gRPC-to-HTTP conversion

### **grafana/grafana** - Multi-Layer Translation
- **`pkg/storage/unified/resource/errors.go`**: Uses `runtime.HTTPStatusFromCode()` to convert gRPC status codes to HTTP responses
- **`pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go`**: Maps specific gRPC codes (InvalidArgument, PermissionDenied, NotFound, Unavailable) to backend status codes
- **`pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/openfga_server.go`**: gRPC-gateway error handlers convert errors to HTTP responses

The complete findings with file paths, symbols, and detailed narrative explanation have been saved to **`/workspace/answer.json`**.
